# Reasoning-Verification Method — Full 1,000-SKU Run

- **Generated:** 2026-06-24 · **Input:** all 1,000 distinct catalog SKUs (`distinct_products_po_1000.csv` via `dual_stage_scored.csv`)
- **Method:** Sonnet 4.6 returns a prediction + an evidence-citing justification; GPT-4o audits whether the *justification* is sound and fully supported by the title (logprobs). **Confidence = P(reasoning is sound)** — the label itself is immaterial.

|---|---|
| rows scored | 1000 (0 errors) |
| reasoning judged sound (>0.85) | **976 (98%)** |
| flagged for review (<=0.85) | **24 (2.4%)** |
| mean confidence | 0.986 |
| predictions: branded / unbranded | 237 / 763 |

**Confidence bands:** <0.50: 10 · 0.50-0.85: 14 · >0.85: 976
